posted:Posted February 5, 2022
msg:Generally speaking, the check-in experience is not good. Objectively speaking, the hotel's hardware facilities and sanitary conditions are not bad, but the hotel's location near the railway is a flaw. My sleep quality is relatively good and I can be woken up by the train several times; second, for customers I said that the first thing you need to stay in a hotel in winter is warmth. As a high-end hotel, in order to save costs, the indoor air conditioner is turned on regularly in winter. Except for the hot wind at night, you need to wear a thick coat in the room at other times. Get up in the morning It's ridiculous to be shivering. Third, there was no electricity when I got up in the morning, and it tripped when I came to check. Of course, this may be an isolated incident, but the combination of multiple incidents greatly affected the comfort of the stay.
        Overall, the hotel's service and management still need to be improved, at least I won't come to stay for the second time.

posted:Posted July 12, 2021
msg:Traveling with children, I specially booked a parent-child room. There are slides and tents in the room. Children like it very much, but this is a very speechless stay. The problems are as follows:
1. The air conditioner is not cooling. I contacted the front desk many times and waited for 40 minutes, but no one came to check the problem. Finally, I said that the general central air conditioner was broken. It will be fine in half an hour, but after one night, it still does not cool.
2. I closed the window before going to bed and found that the window could not be closed. The waiter came to check and confirmed that it was indeed broken, because the child was already asleep at that time, so I asked the waiter to contact the engineer and come back for repairs the next day, but 10 minutes later, the engineer did not bring any tools. Here it is, after checking it out, it still needs to be repaired the next day.
3. The room was changed the next day, but when I entered the room, I found bloody cotton swabs on the ground, which was very disgusting, and I observed carefully. There were pepper chips next to it, and I picked up a child's anti-mosquito bracelet on the ground. This room The sanitation situation is really worrying.
A very disappointing stay! !
